Free Talk

A Word of Wisdom 150

— Autumn Water

The person who laughs the loudest is often not the happiest person.

To shut up, you must first have an open heart.

A man is like a piece of clay in a woman's hand, which can be made round or flat.

Bad habits are like seaweed. If you cannot remove their roots, they will grow more and more each day.

A person who cannot believe in himself can never believe in others.

A married woman can never tell you what her husband said when he proposed, because she has already won and has forgotten the past.

In the past, young women spent all their energy trying to make men inclined to marriage, but modern young women are using their magic to drag men out of marriage.

Love and marriage are purely two different things. Whether a man or a woman has experienced these two things, he or she can never gain any benefit.

People are only a silent gourd to each other. If you can see through the hearts of so-called big shots, you will kill them.

Happy things can never be prolonged. Prolonged happiness is the most distressing thing in the world.

There is no such thing as "lost love" in the world, because true love will never be lost. Lost love is never true love.

Be most careful of the person who hits you without fighting back, because he will neither forgive you nor allow yourself to forgive yourself.

Battlefield Strange News 151

— Yu Yangzhou

A friend of mine followed the camp as a German aide-de-camp translator. He returned home yesterday to visit his relatives and talked about many anecdotes from the battlefield that were not recorded in the newspapers. They are presented as true free talk, perhaps for the people in the South to hear.

My friend said that the Central Army and the Northwest Army were confronting each other in Lanfeng and Tushan for several months. The advances and retreats have caused countless casualties among the people, but there has been no progress. Lanfeng has always been known as a natural barrier, a screen for Zheng and Luo. Therefore, Feng's army relied on the perilous terrain to defend to the death. It is estimated that there are seven lines of defense, planned by Russian military officers. The strength of its defense is no less than Nankou. After the Central Army captured Guide, the commander-in-chief stationed in Liuhe, General Jiang, consulted the German aide-de-camp. The German advised Chiang Kai-shek not to attack the main force of Feng's army, as it would be difficult to achieve great success and only waste real strength. He instructed his subordinates to work hard to attack, and the brave and skilled Central Army broke through five lines of defense. However, due to the strong defenses, landmines, and artillery fire, the remaining two lines were difficult to cross. According to the German, this method was originally created by General Hindenburg. The Russians can build seven lines of defense, and the Germans can build nine. The frontal defense cannot be broken by any sacrifice. It is necessary to use artillery fire to suppress the front and attack both sides with flanking forces to be effective. However, this requires several times the strength of the enemy army to be successful. This shows that the precision and effectiveness of Western firearms in attack and defense are truly astonishing. Recalling our country, I cannot help but shudder.

The Central Army treats the enemy equally, regardless of their origins. However, the cruelty of Feng's army towards the enemy is beyond imagination. It is said that if a Central Army soldier is wounded on the front line and cannot be carried back, Feng orders his subordinates to behead him and leave his body on the battlefield, or to kill him if he has lost his ability to resist. Feng smiled and said that this would be enough to intimidate the opponent's soldiers. This statement from a Feng's army prisoner is said to be reliable.

The daredevil corps of Feng's army are brave and unstoppable. It is said that they often come at night, waving a large flag with one hand, the sound of the wind enough to repel bullets. With the other hand, they hold a broadsword, rolling on the ground and rushing forward. A slight carelessness allows them to break through the line of fire. Moreover, they are hidden in the tall sorghum and wheat fields in the summer, making them even more difficult to defend against. Even with firearms, it is difficult to hit them. Feng's army relies on this as a weapon for attacks. A martial arts expert from Zhejiang, Li, suggested to the headquarters that the "Seven Killing Spear" is the only good method to defeat the broadsword corps. The method is very simple, requiring only seven hands to break the sword. It is unknown whether it will be adopted.

Strange Tales of Dream Plum 152

— Liu Mingyang

Yesterday, I read in "Free Talk" that Mr. Wang Meiju said that there are women in Hangzhou with flower-like patterns, which can be called a strange appearance. But I have heard my friend, the famous painter Ma Qizhou from Shanghai, say that his daughter also has an extraordinary quality. She has a plum blossom on her chest, which can be said to be unique. Therefore, I write this down to add to "Free Talk."

Mr. Ma is a famous scholar from Sichuan. His wife became pregnant before the end of the Xuantong era. On the eve of her delivery, his mother-in-law dreamed of a brocade robe covered with plum blossoms painted by Mr. Ma. She wanted to blame him, but Grandpa Baozhen said it was a wonderful embellishment. The next afternoon, his wife gave birth to a daughter with a cinnabar dot on her chest. After a month, when she was bathed, it was clearly a five-petaled red plum blossom. The stamens of the flower were complete, with the upper half of the moon colored like rouge and the lower half colored like cinnabar. It can be said to be extraordinary. Therefore, she was named Luomei. Also, when this girl was still in swaddling clothes and not yet able to speak clearly, if someone asked about the flower, she would point to her chest. As she grew older, she became intelligent and handsome. She learned to read and never forgot what she had seen. Therefore, the whole family loved her dearly. She is now married to the Jin family. Such a natural anomaly, confirmed in a dream, is truly a strange thing (paid).

Record of Talking About Tigers Turns Pale 153

— Zhou Yuanqi

Zhang Ze, courtesy name Shanzai, is from Neijiang, Sichuan. He is skilled in Zheng Qian's three perfections. He once raised a tiger. The tiger was greedy and Zhang Ze fed it large pieces of fat pork every day. After it was full, he released its iron rope and let it into the deep ravine. Soon, wind would rise as if it were angry or drunk, and it would roar and dance in the valleys, creating unusual sights. When it was hungry, he would put fat pork in a cage, and the tiger would wag its tail and approach it, as if respecting its master. Throughout history, many tiger painters have resembled dogs. Nature painters can only convey the outward appearance of the tiger and cannot capture its true nature. Only Zhang Ze, who has raised tigers for many years, is proficient in painting tigers and is therefore nicknamed the "Tiger Obsessed." One day, Zhang Ze invited messengers to his residence, Da Feng Studio, and showed them a book. He saw that it was titled "Twelve Beauties of Jinling" by Zeng Nongran. The messenger said to Zhang Ze, "You have never liked to create beautiful works of the boudoir. Are you now also imitating the appearance of children?" Zhang Ze said, "Tiger ears." The messenger was greatly shocked and turned pale. Looking at it, it was indeed twelve tigers. Some were crouching, some were standing, some were drinking thirstily, some were angry, and some were charming, showing extreme variations. The inscriptions were filled with romantic words, all with imaginative ideas. On the walls were paintings of tigers, some as large as ten feet and some as small as several feet, with claws dancing and teeth bared, and groups of tigers fighting for food, seemingly symbolizing the worthy officials in power. There were those who hid their heads and showed their tails, wearing tiger skins, symbolizing the even more worthy among the worthy officials in power. The inscription on a painting of a crouching tiger read, "When the fierce tiger is mentioned, those who hear it turn pale." I have heard that fierce tigers lie in deep mountains, but now fierce tigers are in the public eye. Alas, the road is difficult. Are you good at satirizing the world?" Zhang Ze heard this and smiled. Wang Yiting, the man from Bailong Mountain, once painted a portrait of Zhang Ze with a tangled beard flying, his form resembling a tiger, and inscribed it with the words, "Knowing that you are accustomed to conveying the spirit of the tiger, painting the appearance of the tiger as if it were your own body, born with a tiger's beard and a majestic appearance, depicting the tiger's power with all your spirit." Zhang Ze's majestic appearance is indeed like that of a mountain lord. Zhang Ze once worked as a scribe under Zeng Nongran, the master of the You Tian Xi Hai Studio. With the talent of a magistrate, he retired to pursue painting and poetry, which are also deeply rooted. He is truly a unique figure in the art world.

Postscript to the Mute Love Lawsuit 154

— Shen Hengzhuang

After the mute love case involving Lin Jim and Wu Airong occurred, in order to maintain their livelihood and save face with relatives and friends, the loving couple simultaneously joined the Current Affairs Film Company as actors. The company took the opportunity to produce the film "Mute Lovers," with Lin and Wu as the main characters and Chen Zhuomin as the director. The plot is a true depiction of the main actors' experiences. Filming began three months ago and has now been completed. Lin and Wu receive a monthly salary of one hundred yuan, which solves their livelihood problems. Now that the lawsuit has ended, the film starring Lin and Wu will also be screened at the Central Theater. In order to increase its appeal, the company has obtained Lin and Wu's consent to perform on stage at the same time as the film. However, since Lin is mute, the problem of performing is particularly difficult. Therefore, the responsible personnel of the company consulted Mr. Zhou Shixun. Zhou is good at planning and created a mute drama entitled "Unspeakable Secret," in which Lin plays a heartbroken musician and Wu plays a maiden. The plot is extremely subtle, and the scenery and costumes are quite beautiful. However, Zhou, in order to demand the actors' movements and expressions, specially invited Mr. Tao Zhongcheng to direct. For days, the loving couple rushed around Carter Road, extremely busy. Sometimes, Wu Airong even brought the baby Lin Jim to rehearsals so she could breastfeed him. It is also heard that on the day of the performance, Wu Airong will sing a love song, with lyrics composed by the famous musician Pan Boying, the words of which express the utmost grief. Therefore, in addition to singing lullabies, Wu Airong's boudoir life has added another kind of mood.

Travel Notes from Nanyang (48) 155

— Linghua

The local natives here are simple in knowledge, kind in behavior, and rich in ancient customs. There are absolutely no cases of theft or robbery, but I fear that the arrival of Chinese people will gradually disrupt this. In the past, the Mongol disciple Wu Fuyuan often talked about this. The Mongols used earthen carts to push silver ingots, loaded with straw, and placed them in the wilderness without fear of bandits or robbery. Also, Mrs. Huang Zhaogui of Singapore told me that she was at the house of a local gentry. The gentry returned from overseas with many pearls and showed them to guests. The glass windows around his room were wide open, with no one guarding them. Even the Malays gathered to watch. Mrs. Huang privately thought that if there were a robbery, she would also be implicated. But in fact, the morality of the Nanyang natives is very high, and there is absolutely no such thing to worry about. However, in recent years, the number of Chinese people has increased, and kidnapping has gradually spread to the South, which is worrying for the future.

Seeing the peace and tranquility of the Malay villages, I wrote a poem to express its meaning:

From Klang to Kuala Lumpur, seeing the Nanyang villages, it proves the culture of today's Tock Workers and the ancient Lao Zhuang.

From Klang to Kuala Lumpur, it is about sixty miles. The car or train takes an hour to arrive. Along the way, the rubber trees are high and low, filling the slopes. The branches reach the sky, shielding the sun. The green shade is cool and breezy. In the midst are the houses of the natives, a few feet off the ground. Red tiles and thatched roofs, clean and beautiful. Three or five families are shaded by sparse bamboo. Red men and green women live in peace until old age. White cows of Indian breed are rarely seen, along with chickens, dogs, and pigs. Banana trees and phoenix tails, purple flowers winding. Or there are pigeons and doves raised on the hillside by the water's edge. Railways and cars pass through, carrying loads and singing in harmony. Never hearing of turmoil or separation, being full is all that matters. I sigh at the well-governed small country with few people. Reading and still discussing what is difficult, I begin to prove the meaning of Lao Zhuang. Non-action leads to non-disturbance. The highest good is like flowing water, plowing and forgetting the emperor's power. Monkeys in hats destroy nests. Allow this long-term existence. Yao and Shun are true chaff. The setting sun and the cow's back are steady. The world is a worn-out shoe. The old man Xu Xing is a disciple, and the monarch and subject become waste paper. In the high heavens and thick earth, leisurely contentment is enough. Why use the sick Xia Kui and the shouldered foreheads? Yan Guang and Tao Yuanming have no remaining sons for a thousand years. This learning is now greatly illuminated. New villages replace cities. Tockes and Weirs' benevolence become fortifications. The early people's villages of Nanyang rely on this archaeological discovery. Advanced savages also. Above is no free reason, the forest is true life. Men and women enjoy themselves together. The great chaos in the world is what is contended for in the court and the market. Power cuts off people's heads and capital sucks people's marrow. Potted flowers dry up and pond fish, how can they reach old age? Classes become blind fights and false pleasures. I travel to Guilin, marveling at the beautiful mountains and waters. Immigrants can number in the millions, holding hoes and carrying plows. I will call out to Jieni and begin plowing from now on.

Warmth in My Heart (276) 156

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 14: Verdant Bamboo and Mottled Doors, Her Heart Breaks; Red Lotus Fragrance, a Woman is Alone.

Since Zhang Yiqing lived with this unofficial old man, it was like a fish in water. Not only was their sexual harmony like a fish in water, but he was also like a fish in water economically. Because he was a capable man in the Shanghai business world, he could be called a genius. His methods of flirting with wealthy Shanghai merchants were as clever as those of Shanghai women. In the past, he inevitably had some empty runs, but it was not easy to form this situation. Now that he had a female army as a support team, it was like he was in the middle of an offensive and suddenly a reinforcement joined, naturally boosting his power. Zhang Yiqing's position was then booming. However, this woman was not weak either. As the saying goes, with wealth and power, since she had given Zhang Yiqing many rights, Zhang Yiqing had to fulfill some obligations to her. At that time, there was naturally a condition, and the most important condition was that Zhang Yiqing had to be a loyal believer to her. Not only should he treat the old man from Ningbo as nothing, but he also had to unify his thoughts and not allow any more random thoughts. Zhang Yiqing was very willing to swear when he first took office and received his duties, saying that anyone with different ambitions should be subjected to the old man's most severe punishment. However, this kind of male-female combination was like plating something with electricity. In the first few years, there was still enough electricity. Gradually, this young old man became a real old man. The youthful layer of electricity gradually faded away, and the two could no longer generate much electricity. If this friend's wife still possessed huge sums of money and did not relax at all, and Zhang Yiqing himself had no power to move, then he would have to submit to the old man and become a lifelong dresser slave. However, he had his own ability to move and felt that if he continued to be bound by others, how long would life be? What was the use of money if he could not enjoy himself in time? Moreover, no matter what kind of spouse lasted for more than ten years, love gradually decreased and conflicts gradually increased. When they were on good terms, everyone did not take a joke seriously. At that time, a great wind arose from the end of the duckweed, and often a completely unrelated word caused a great quarrel. Even if the quarrels of young couples were intense, when they were nestled in bed, peace filled the air. When studying physiology, they no longer debated about ethics. When they got older, it was not so easy to reconcile. For example, the woman Zhang Yiqing was messing with thought that she had brought the money in the first place and that Zhang Yiqing had become proud because of her help, which had cultivated a arrogant habit. Naturally, her temper got worse as she got older. Not only was she a closed-door emperor, but she sometimes scolded Zhang Yiqing. Zhang Yiqing was certainly a little annoyed by her, but under her accumulated power, he could not help but be a little afraid of her.

The situation for guest traders was: Jiangxi urgently took in 40 bales, Tianjin 25 bales, Hankou 15 bales, Sichuan 10 bales, inland areas 45 bales, and miscellaneous traders 35 bales.

Cotton Market Shaky and Unstable 163

The cotton market situation is unfavorable. American cotton is extremely weak, with new low prices appearing for the October and December contracts. However, the local market sentiment has not declined significantly because some bulls are holding on tightly, expecting higher prices. However, one firm's previous purchases now face an unfavorable environment and are secretly being released. Furthermore, the exchange rate is shifting, and Indian cotton is taking the opportunity to enter the market at lower prices. Considering foreign cotton, the future is still difficult to stabilize.

Han-Mark (漢標) trends are sparse. The opening price of the Han-Mark market followed the downward trend of foreign cotton. However, the bulls held on tightly, and prices for all months only fell by one or two mace. In the afternoon, the yarn market was unfavorable, and the situation slightly weakened, with prices for all months falling by one mace. The total turnover for the day was 43,000 bales. Shen Yu bought 2,500 bales, Heng De 2,700 bales, Feng 3,200 bales, Yi Yu 1,800 bales, and others 1,000 to 1,300 bales. Tian Chang sold 5,700 bales, Da Feng 2,600 bales, Rui Da 2,700 bales, Mao Ji 2,000 bales, and others 900 to 2,800 bales. The closing prices for Han-Mark are recorded below:

American Cotton Was Firm Last Week 166

A telegram from New York on the 12th reports on the cotton market during the week, stating that the government's estimate report this week was approximately 300,000 bales higher than the public's expectations. As a result, bulls closed out their positions, and there were also new sales. However, the downward trend was met with significant absorption. The spot situation did not show weakness, and there was also a hoarding movement in the South. Therefore, the market rebounded after professional buying and short covering. There was relatively little hedging, so the underlying trend was stable. As for the current market action, it entirely depends on the market situation in the South.

Furthermore, the volume of hedge selling is limited, and professional traders are buying futures at limit prices. The negative impact of the Department of Agriculture's report was offset by speculative short covering. Although cooperatives are hoarding large quantities of spot cotton, demand is flat, and yarn mills are still reducing production. Since the release of the Department of Agriculture's report, domestic piece goods trade has become even more stagnant. Grain: The Heshia Rice Market is Weakening 168

Qiaoxi New Japonica is Becoming Scarce

Zhabei: The source of goods arriving yesterday was not much. Ke Xian rice coming by truck was more active. The sales activity on this street is moderate because the market situation on the road inside the city is reported to be stable. Furthermore, there is a continuous supply of imported rice and Yangtze River rice, so people are not optimistic about higher prices. Although appetite is good, purchasing power is tight. The price of Bai Po rice has not fluctuated much because the goods are scarce. The prices of all high and medium grade Japonica rice are the same as the previous market. Several dozen shi of Xixin Japonica rice arrived, and the quality can be described as top-notch. The price is 20 yuan and 5 jiao, which is 5 or 6 jiao more expensive than last year. The supply of Dongxin Japonica rice is becoming even more depleted. Rice mills' willingness to sell remains weak, and the price remains at 18 yuan and a half. New Yang Jian rice is gradually becoming abundant, and the price has weakened by 2 jiao, only at 15 yuan and a bit. New Ke Jian rice arrives in Shanghai in about 20 truckloads every day, and there were slightly more buyers yesterday. Therefore, everyone is taking a short position, so the market price has slightly decreased by 2 or 3 jiao. Top-notch goods are offered at 14 yuan, while the discount on ordinary goods is very substantial. There are very few high-quality Bo Dao rice, and ordinary rice is also scarce. The large market opens at 20 yuan and half, while Bai Yuan rice remains unchanged.

Hunan: The source of goods from Hexia is becoming even more depleted. Although sales are active, transactions are minimal. The large market is extremely quiet. There is a slight supply of medium-grade Broken Japonica rice, and the market is stable. Su Tong goods continue to be offered at 20 yuan to 19 yuan and a half. New Japonica rice is generally hovering. The price of Dongxin Wu rice is the same as in the Zhabei market, at 17 yuan and a half. The price of new Japonica rice from this area is also very stable. The recent arrival of high-quality Bo Dao rice such as Qing Ding Jiao Li from this area has been frequent, so the price is still at the 21 yuan mark. The daily arrival of Yang Jian Xin Jian rice is quite substantial, and the sales seem to be weak. The market surface is slightly soft, and prices are weakening recently.

Tapioca Market Continues to Weaken 169

Yesterday, after the opening of the tapioca market in the morning and afternoon, the market prices for each month uniformly tended to weaken. Because the quoted price of imported wheat flour continued to decrease slightly, at 2, 4 jiao or 1 yuan, people's confidence naturally weakened further. Although manufacturers are still not loosening their grip on the current month, the environment is no longer what it used to be. In the end, it also trended downward. As for the distant months, although the manufacturers' attitude is still mainly firm, they are secretly releasing positions one after another. The major client of a certain major factory is even gradually engaging in wild selling. The only reason is that, according to the manufacturers, the amount of foreign ginseng tapioca flour already ordered by guest traders is not small. With this two-pronged approach, the future situation seems to be increasingly bleak. According to general speculation, the first target for the distant months is to fall to the 2 taels and 4 qian mark. As a result, the current month fell by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, October fell by 1.75 fen, November and December fell by 1.25 fen, January fell by 1.75 fen, and February fell by 2 fen.

Wheat Futures Market Plunges Unceasingly 170

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the market prices for each month uniformly plunged unceasingly. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat flour decreased again, people's confidence was even more discouraged. Furthermore, it was rumored that the manufacturers had already ordered four ships of foreign wheat flour, totaling approximately 10,000 tons or more. The settlement price was either 20 yuan or 29 yuan and 7 jiao and a half. Therefore, the future of the wheat market, in view of the formidable enemy of foreign wheat flour, if this continues, there will be little hope. Therefore, the strength of selling was rarely seen since the new market opened. However, it was heard that this type of foreign wheat flour is the United States government's strategic reserve grain. Standard wheat in that country is still not affordable as such. As a result, the current month fell by another 6 fen compared to the previous day, October and November fell by 5 fen, December fell by 6 fen, January fell by 5 fen, and February fell by 6 fen. The spot wheat market is exceptionally quiet because each factory is still holding on and not dealing. There have been no transactions in the entire city.

North-South Goods: First Batch of New Walnuts Arrives, 7,000 Bags 171

Price Opened at 21 Taels to 20 Taels

The first batch of new walnuts, totaling 7,000 bags, is Changping goods, all personally handled by experienced traders. The color and quality are still good. Because it is the first time seeing new goods, the trend is brisk, selling at 21 taels to 20 taels. It is also heard that land prices in Tianjin have tightened, and it may be difficult to loosen them in the short term.

Silk and Tea: Wuxi Autumn Cocoons Have Opened for Weighing 172

Autumn Cocoons in Wuxi Have Generally Reached the Market. The cocoon markets established by various silk factories have begun collecting cocoons on the 10th. They were officially opened for weighing on the 12th. This year's autumn cocoons are of ordinary quality, and the cocoon harvest is about 70-80%. Currently, the autumn cocoons from the Northeast Road are priced at 47-48 yuan per dan. The opening of the cocoon markets on the Southwest Road is later. It is heard that the cocoon price may be slightly higher than the Northeast Road.

Gaozhuang Zhenmei's Sales to Europe Have Improved 173

Yesterday, the Yingzhuang Jinjiang foreign trade industry of Gaozhuang Zhenmei green tea in Wuyuan has greatly increased its sourcing. The intention to purchase from Baochang Yongxing and other firms has also become stronger. The selling price has shown a slight firming trend. However, the sales of Zhenmei tea from middle and low grades seem to be stagnant. Since the suspension of Russian trade for Gongxi, the accumulation has increased daily. The trend in the tea market must depend on whether or not the Russian trade can be opened.

Shanghai Market

Market News 181

The Qingyise Restaurant at the intersection of Sanma Road and Zhejiang Road proclaims that the chef Mr. Luo currently employed by this restaurant has studied Cantonese cuisine for more than 30 years. His superb cooking skills have long been praised by customers. Therefore, since he took over, the business has been thriving. The one yuan and two jiao special set meal is particularly popular. In order to facilitate lunchtime and late-night dining for all sectors, the restaurant has specially added various economical dishes, as well as noodles and porridge, with prices ranging from 1 jiao and 5 fen to 2 or 3 jiao. Recently, those from all walks of life who have tried it have expressed their satisfaction.

The Yanhua Restaurant, opposite the Dangui Stage at Sima Road, proclaims that the restaurant's preserved meat technician has more than 20 years of experience. The various Cantonese preserved meats he produces are particularly skillful, ranking first in Shanghai. The taste is sweet, fragrant, and palatable, and the ingredients are all selected from top-quality sources, which has long been praised by all sectors. Therefore, the annual sales volume is quite high. The most famous products are duck liver sausage, rose sausage, duck legs, and duck breast. Currently, duck legs and duck breast are on the market, with duck legs priced at 3 jiao and 3 fen per leg, and duck breast priced at 1 jiao and 7 fen per breast. In addition, since autumn, the number of diners in the restaurant's wine and dishes department has increased, and the interior and exterior decorations have been completely renovated. The arrangement is clean, elegant, and extremely satisfactory to customers.

Shanghai Tobacco Company declares that the Creas cigarettes managed by the company have a mellow taste and reasonable prices. They have been popular in Europe and America for many years. Since they became popular in China, they have also enjoyed a long-standing reputation, and famous people and professionals have regarded them as the ultimate product. As a result, sales are brisk and demand exceeds supply. In order to reward the customers' favor and expectations, the company has telegraphed the London headquarters to urge shipment, and a large batch will arrive in Shanghai soon.

The Sanxin Company on Peng Road, North Sichuan Road, declares that the company has been established for more than three years. In addition to selling daily necessities, its most famous products are suits and shirts. There is a complete range of clothing for spring, summer, autumn, and winter, with more than a hundred styles and thousands of pieces in various sizes, priced from one yuan to several yuan. Most of the suits sold in various suit shops on the market are its products. The tailoring is suitable and the prices are low. Therefore, business and academic circles are happy to purchase and use them. At the West Lake Exposition last year, the company once displayed the Three-Character brand underwear and the Great King brand shirts for people to visit, and it was recognized as a rare item in the shirt industry. After examination by Zhang Jingjiang, the president of the association, and Zhu Jiahua, the director of the examination committee, a silver medal and a first-class certificate No. 725 of the West Lake Exposition were specially awarded. In addition to sending a letter of thanks for this commendation, the company is making more efforts to improve the quality of its products in order to live up to the enthusiasm of those who love and use domestic goods.

Page 22

Theater News 182

The Central Grand Theater announces that the newly emerging film star Zhang Yuqing has entered the film industry as a star due to her beauty and cleverness. Her debut film, "Circus Girl," is directed by Wang Cilong. In addition to Zhang Yuqing, the leading actors also include Zhou Wenzhu. Wang Cilong also plays the villain in the play. This film has been in production for a long time, but has not yet been publicly screened in Shanghai's cinemas. It has achieved great success in other cities. The expressions of lust and flesh are completely realistic and vivid. It is said that this film will be publicly screened at this grand theater starting tomorrow. In addition to the film, Zheng Zhengqiu's newly compiled play "General Dog Meat Bids Farewell to His Concubine" will be performed on stage. The performers include Tan Zhiyuan, Tianhen, and more than twenty others. There is singing and dancing, making it extremely lively. The scenery is specially made and has a strong artistic concept. It is a rare opportunity to have a famous film and excellent play performed at the same time without raising ticket prices.

The Peking Opera Department of the Commercial Press Workers' Union announces that the department has been established for more than ten years. It has rehearsed over a hundred times and has repeatedly received praise from all walks of life. It is scheduled to hold its 134th rehearsal at the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce at 1:00 PM on the 21st of this month. The program includes "Wu Jia Po" by Mei Hexuan, "Hong Luan Xi" by Li Jinsheng, "Autumn Hu Teases His Wife" by Zhu Bingli, "Falling Horse Lake" by Peng Jun, "Crossing the River to the Banquet" by Li Changjian and Luo Yusheng, "Tianba Worships the Mountain" by Li Zhengang and Shen Bin, "Farewell to the Cave" by Liu Aoqi, "Famen Temple" by Yan Zhongli and Cao Guoliang, "Nine-Bend Bridge" by Xu Zhenjiang and Zhang Zhijun, and "Wu Zhaoguan" by Chen Meifang and Shen Yihe. All the costumes are brand new, and many famous ticket holders have borrowed costumes from famous actors privately, making them even more outstanding. Recent rehearsals have been very successful, and Chen Meifang's Qingyi and Huadan roles are excellent in both singing and acting. She is very much like the successor of Mei Lanfang and will add a lot of color at that time.

Shen Bao Pictorial Weekly

(1) The main entrance of the Chinese Pavilion at the Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition.

(2) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the Chinese Pavilion at the Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition.

— (Xu Shiqi)

(3) Members of the Chinese Pavilion participating in the Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition. Standing in the center is the Commissioner-General Min Yi, to his right is the Deputy Representative Liu Xichang and Secretary-General Nong Ruhui.

— (Xu Shiqi)

(4) The International Pavilion of the Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition, with the Chinese Pavilion located inside.

(5) The corridor of the Chinese Pavilion at the Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition.

(6) Mr. Wendervelde, representing the Belgian government to participate in the opening of the Chinese Pavilion at the Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition. He is a leader in the Belgian society. Mr. Feng Hua of the Chinese Central Research Institute has already returned to Beiping with his wife on September 3rd.

— (Xu Shiqi)

The Belgian Independence Centennial Exposition was held at that time. One exhibition belonged to the various sub-countries and had a maritime nature, while the other, held in Liège, pertained to the industrial, commercial, and educational nature of the various countries. The Liège Exposition was further divided into northern and southern sections. The Chinese Pavilion was located in the northern International Pavilion, occupying an area of approximately 300 cubic meters. Because the International Pavilion had a roof and a cement floor, the Chinese Pavilion did not build a separate pavilion in order to be practical and economical. Although the area was not very large, the layout was appropriate and the decoration was magnificent and worth seeing. It was divided into three sections: agriculture, education, and industry and commerce. Two types of catalogs were printed, one being a general catalog and the other being an art catalog. In addition to inviting foreigners, the Chinese Pavilion officially opened on June 16th. Mr. Wendervelde, the former Minister of Foreign Affairs of the Belgian government, participated, and Chinese and foreign participants were given tea, a copy of the Three Principles of the People, and four Exposition postcards. There was a banquet in the evening, and on August 2nd, the Belgian principal also moved to visit and add to the pavilion. The various items displayed in the pavilion were immediately praised and praised, and some people entrusted the purchase of herbal medicine and other items, showing their love for it. It can be seen that the exposition is scheduled to close in October. The representative of our country, Mr. Min Yi, will take the route through the United States in September to return to China. The remaining people will have to return after the end of the conference. Ruhui recognized.

She participated in the International Women's Conference and spoke on the national government's newly enacted laws for the development of women's rights and the rapid progress of Chinese women in recent years, attracting the attention of the audience.
